- 中文速读：内容聚焦教育、学习或高校场景，适合关注技术变化如何影响学生、教师和家庭的日常选择。

- 摘要：English has many patterns. Learning and mastering these patterns can help you improve your writing and speaking skills. Today's common pattern is the transitive verb pattern. There are several types of transitive verbs, but they all have one thing in common: a direct object.
- 中文速读：内容聚焦教育、学习或高校场景，适合关注技术变化如何影响学生、教师和家庭的日常选择。

## 365. Academic Writing: Common Sentence Patterns, Part One
- 来源：VOA Learning English - Everyday Grammar
- 发布时间：2025-01-23T22:05:41+00:00
- 优先级分数：15
- 推荐级别：观察中
- 是否重复：False
- 重复原因：无
- 首次推送日期：无
- 标签：观察
- 链接：https://learningenglish.voanews.com/a/everyday-grammar-common-patterns/3988378.html
- 摘要：Today on Everyday Grammar, we explore two grammatical structures that you will see often in academic writing. These structures are used to evaluate ideas and evaluate actions. Although common in academic writing, you might not want to use these structures in other types of writing.
